• 7201. Canonical Path Map Overview
  7202. Path Map Philosophy
  7203. Path Map Governance
  7204. Path Map Quality Standards
  7205. Path Map Stability Rules
  7206. Path Map Translation Rules
  7207. Path Map Resolution Rules
  7208. Path Map Logging Rules
  7209. Path Map Security Rules
  7210. Canonical Path Map Index
  7211. macOS Canonical Path Map
  7212. HOME_FOLDER -> /Users/{username}
  7213. DESKTOP_FOLDER -> /Users/{username}/Desktop
  7214. DOCUMENTS_FOLDER -> /Users/{username}/Documents
  7215. DOWNLOADS_FOLDER -> /Users/{username}/Downloads
  7216. PICTURES_FOLDER -> /Users/{username}/Pictures
  7217. MUSIC_FOLDER -> /Users/{username}/Music
  7218. VIDEOS_FOLDER -> /Users/{username}/Movies
  7219. PUBLIC_FOLDER -> /Users/{username}/Public
  7220. TRASH_FOLDER -> /Users/{username}/.Trash
  7221. macOS System Paths
  7222. ROOT_FOLDER -> /
  7223. USERS_FOLDER -> /Users
  7224. APPLICATIONS_FOLDER -> /Applications
  7225. SYSTEM_FOLDER -> /System
  7226. LIBRARY_FOLDER -> /Library
  7227. CONFIG_FOLDER -> /Users/{username}/.config or /Users/{username}/Library/Preferences
  7228. CACHE_FOLDER -> /Users/{username}/Library/Caches
  7229. LOGS_FOLDER -> /Users/{username}/Library/Logs
  7230. TEMP_FOLDER -> /private/tmp or app-local temp paths
  7231. Linux Canonical Path Map
  7232. HOME_FOLDER -> /home/{username}
  7233. DESKTOP_FOLDER -> /home/{username}/Desktop
  7234. DOCUMENTS_FOLDER -> /home/{username}/Documents
  7235. DOWNLOADS_FOLDER -> /home/{username}/Downloads
  7236. PICTURES_FOLDER -> /home/{username}/Pictures
  7237. MUSIC_FOLDER -> /home/{username}/Music
  7238. VIDEOS_FOLDER -> /home/{username}/Videos
  7239. PUBLIC_FOLDER -> /home/{username}/Public
  7240. TRASH_FOLDER -> distro-specific user trash paths
  7241. Linux System Paths
  7242. ROOT_FOLDER -> /
  7243. USERS_FOLDER -> /home
  7244. APPLICATIONS_FOLDER -> /usr/share/applications or /opt
  7245. SYSTEM_FOLDER -> /usr, /etc, /var
  7246. LIBRARY_FOLDER -> /usr/share and app-specific data roots
  7247. CONFIG_FOLDER -> /home/{username}/.config
  7248. CACHE_FOLDER -> /home/{username}/.cache
  7249. LOGS_FOLDER -> /var/log or app-local logs
  7250. TEMP_FOLDER -> /tmp
  7251. Windows Canonical Path Map
  7252. HOME_FOLDER -> C:\Users\{username}
  7253. DESKTOP_FOLDER -> C:\Users\{username}\Desktop
  7254. DOCUMENTS_FOLDER -> C:\Users\{username}\Documents
  7255. DOWNLOADS_FOLDER -> C:\Users\{username}\Downloads
  7256. PICTURES_FOLDER -> C:\Users\{username}\Pictures
  7257. MUSIC_FOLDER -> C:\Users\{username}\Music
  7258. VIDEOS_FOLDER -> C:\Users\{username}\Videos
  7259. PUBLIC_FOLDER -> C:\Users\Public or C:\Users\{username}\Public
  7260. TRASH_FOLDER -> Recycle Bin abstraction, not a normal path
  7261. Windows System Paths
  7262. ROOT_FOLDER -> C:\
  7263. USERS_FOLDER -> C:\Users
  7264. APPLICATIONS_FOLDER -> C:\Program Files
  7265. SYSTEM_FOLDER -> C:\Windows
  7266. LIBRARY_FOLDER -> C:\ProgramData
  7267. CONFIG_FOLDER -> C:\Users\{username}\AppData\Roaming
  7268. CACHE_FOLDER -> C:\Users\{username}\AppData\Local
  7269. LOGS_FOLDER -> app-specific local or program data paths
  7270. TEMP_FOLDER -> %TEMP% and %TMP%
  7271. Mobile And Tablet Canonical Maps
  7272. iOS HOME_FOLDER -> app sandbox root abstraction
  7273. iOS DOCUMENTS_FOLDER -> app documents directory
  7274. iOS DOWNLOADS_FOLDER -> Files app / provider abstraction
  7275. iPadOS DESKTOP_FOLDER -> no true desktop, Files app approximation
  7276. Android HOME_FOLDER -> app sandbox or user storage abstraction
  7277. Android DOWNLOADS_FOLDER -> standard Downloads provider
  7278. Android DOCUMENTS_FOLDER -> Documents provider abstraction
  7279. Mobile TRASH_FOLDER -> provider-specific, often abstracted
  7280. Mobile Path Map Index
  7281. Browser And Web Canonical Maps
  7282. HOME_FOLDER -> browser user-space abstraction
  7283. DOCUMENTS_FOLDER -> upload picker abstraction
  7284. DOWNLOADS_FOLDER -> browser-managed downloads
  7285. APPDATA_FOLDER -> IndexedDB / OPFS / local storage abstraction
  7286. CACHE_FOLDER -> Cache API / browser cache
  7287. TEMP_FOLDER -> transient blob and session storage
  7288. SHARED_FOLDER -> cloud-provider picker abstraction
  7289. BROWSER_PATH_RESOLUTION_RULES
  7290. Browser Path Map Index
  7291. BlackRoad Example Canonical Paths
  7292. BR_HOME On macOS -> /Users/{username}
  7293. BR_HOME On Linux -> /home/{username}
  7294. BR_HOME On Windows -> C:\Users\{username}
  7295. BR_MEMORY On macOS -> ~/.blackroad or configured memory path
  7296. BR_WORKSPACE On macOS -> /Users/{username} or project root
  7297. BR_DOCS On macOS -> /Users/{username}/docs when local convention exists
  7298. BR_PRODUCTS On macOS -> /Users/{username}/services when local convention exists

• 10601. Filled Template Overview
  10602. Filled Template Philosophy
  10603. Filled Template Governance
  10604. Filled Template Quality Standards
  10605. Filled Template Stability Rules
  10606. Filled Template Validation Rules
  10607. Filled Template Logging Rules
  10608. Filled Template Security Rules
  10609. Filled Template Portability Rules
  10610. Filled Template Index
  10611. 0001-Master-Index.md Filled Text
  10612. # BlackRoad Operating Binder
  10613. ## Purpose
  10614. This binder is the canonical operating system for BlackRoad governance, structure, finance, compliance,
     products, and execution.
  10615. ## Volume Map
  10616. 01 Constitution | 02 Institution | 03 Products And Markets | 04 Finance And Treasury | 05 Compliance And
     Trust | 06 Operations And Execution | 07 Filesystem And Infrastructure
  10617. ## Canonical Source Rule
  10618. When duplicate files exist, the binder copy is the canonical control copy after review and naming
     normalization.
  10619. ## Review Status
  10620. Status: Draft / Owner: Alexa / Last Review: YYYY-MM-DD
  10621. 0005-Change-Log.md Filled Text
  10622. # BlackRoad Change Log
  10623. ## Entry Format
  10624. Date | Owner | File | Change Summary | Reason | Approval Status | Follow-Up
  10625. ## First Entry Example
  10626. YYYY-MM-DD | Alexa | 0161-Stock-Ledger.xlsx | Created initial ledger | Required for canonical records |
     Pending | Verify certificate numbering
  10627. ## Logging Rule
  10628. Every structural, legal, ownership, or governance document change should be logged here before or at time
     of finalization.
  10629. ## Review Rule
  10630. Review this file during annual binder refresh and after major financing, trust, or subsidiary changes.
  10631. 0151-Trust-Summary.md Filled Text
  10632. # Trust Summary
  10633. ## Trust Identity
  10634. Trust Name: [Insert exact trust name]
  10635. Trust Date: [Insert date]
  10636. Trustee: Alexa Louise Amundson
  10637. Successor Trustee: [Insert successor trustee]
  10638. ## Corporate Relationship
  10639. This trust is intended to hold shares of BlackRoad OS, Inc. at the shareholder level and does not replace
     the corporation itself.
  10640. ## Open Questions
  10641. 0153-Trust-Transfer-Checklist.md Filled Text
  10642. # Trust Transfer Checklist
  10643. ## Preconditions
  10644. - Confirm exact legal trust name matches trust documents
  10645. - Confirm current stock certificate holder name
  10646. - Confirm transfer restrictions under RSPA and related records
  10647. ## Transfer Steps
  10648. - Determine whether board consent is required
  10649. - Reissue or annotate certificate as needed
  10650. - Update stock ledger and cap table immediately after transfer
  10651. 0167-Equity-Issuance-Checklist.md Filled Text
  10652. # Equity Issuance Checklist
  10653. ## Issuance Context
  10654. Recipient: [Name]
  10655. Security Type: [Common / Preferred / Restricted Stock / Option]
  10656. Shares or Units: [Insert amount]
  10657. ## Required Steps
  10658. - Board approval adopted
  10659. - Consideration documented
  10660. - Ledger and cap table updated
  10661. 0411-Banking-Accounts-Register.md Filled Text
  10662. # Banking Accounts Register
  10663. ## Purpose
  10664. Track every bank, brokerage, treasury, and custody relationship used by BlackRoad and its subsidiaries.
  10665. ## Required Fields
  10666. Institution | Account Name | Last Four | Entity Owner | Purpose | Authorized Signers | Status | Notes
  10667. ## Control Rule
  10668. No account should exist without a linked entity owner, defined purpose, and current signer review.
  10669. ## Review Cadence
  10670. Review monthly for active accounts and annually for the full binder.
  10671. 0468-Tax-Calendar.md Filled Text
  10672. # Tax Calendar
  10673. ## Delaware
  10674. - Annual report due by March 1
  10675. - Franchise tax due by March 1
  10676. ## Minnesota
  10677. - Annual business renewal due by December 31 if registered
  10678. - Corporate return timing follows applicable tax-year filing deadlines
  10679. ## Federal
  10680. - Form 1120 due according to current IRS corporate filing calendar
  10681. 0561-Annual-Compliance-Checklist.md Filled Text
  10682. # Annual Compliance Checklist
  10683. ## Parent Good Standing
  10684. - Confirm Delaware annual report filed
  10685. - Confirm Delaware franchise tax paid
  10686. - Confirm registered agent active
  10687. ## Minnesota
  10688. - Confirm foreign qualification remains active if required
  10689. - Confirm annual renewal filed
  10690. ## Records
  10691. 0007-Document-Register.xlsx Filled Text
  10692. Workbook Columns
  10693. Document ID | Canonical Filename | Current Location | Canonical Binder Path | Owner | Status | Last
     Reviewed | Notes
  10694. Status Values
  10695. Have Local | Have Drive | Missing | Placeholder Created | Needs Review | Canonicalized
  10696. Purpose Rule
  10697. Every important legal, tax, governance, treasury, trust, and equity file should appear in this register.
  10698. Maintenance Rule
  10699. Update the register whenever a file is moved, renamed, replaced, or designated as canonical.

  12409. Work Queue Portability Rules
  12410. Best-Order Work Queue Index
  12411. First Click Sequence
  12412. Create root binder tree
  12413. Create subfolders for constitution, equity, trust, finance, and compliance
  12414. Create placeholder receipt and return folders
  12415. Create markdown control files
  12416. Create workbook control files
  12417. Add starter content to markdown files
  12418. Add headers to workbooks
  12419. Save all files under canonical names immediately
  12420. First Click Index
  12421. Second Click Sequence
  12422. Copy local signed certificate into canonical path
  12423. Copy local approved certificate into canonical path
  12424. Copy local bylaws into canonical path provisionally
  12425. Copy local secretary certificate into canonical path
  12426. Copy local initial board action into canonical path provisionally
  12427. Copy local stockholder consent into canonical path provisionally
  12428. Copy local stock certificate into canonical path
  12429. Copy local stock assignment into canonical path
  12430. Second Click Index
  12431. Third Click Sequence
  12432. Copy local SS-4 into canonical path
  12433. Import Drive RSPA into canonical path
  12434. Import Drive 83(b) into canonical path
  12435. Import Drive indemnification agreement into canonical path
  12436. Import Drive CIIAA into canonical path
  12437. Import Drive joint escrow instructions into canonical path
  12438. Mark missing EIN confirmation as placeholder
  12439. Mark missing Delaware receipts as placeholders
  12440. Third Click Index
  12441. Fourth Click Sequence
  12442. Populate document register with local files
  12443. Populate document register with Drive files
  12444. Populate document register with missing placeholder rows
  12445. Mark duplicates for bylaws, board action, and consent
  12446. Set review date to 2026-04-09
  12447. Populate signer register with founder authority row
  12448. Populate compliance deadline register with baseline deadlines
  12449. Save and lock register structure
  12450. Fourth Click Index
  12451. Fifth Click Sequence
  12452. Build stock ledger workbook structure
  12453. Build cap table workbook structure
  12454. Add founder placeholder row to ledger
  12455. Add founder placeholder rows to cap table sheets
  12456. Mark exact share count pending
  12457. Mark exact issue date pending
  12458. Mark vesting and repurchase terms pending
  12459. Link source references to board action and stock certificate
  12460. Fifth Click Index
  12461. Sixth Click Sequence
  12462. Compare local and Drive bylaws side by side
  12463. Compare local and Drive board action side by side
  12464. Compare local and Drive stockholder consent side by side
  12465. Choose cleaner complete signed copy for each
  12466. Update document register with final canonical decision
  12467. Archive or label non-canonical copies
  12468. Log duplicate-resolution notes in change log
  12469. Refresh review dates
  12470. Sixth Click Index
  12471. Seventh Click Sequence
  12472. Extract exact founder share count from certificate and RSPA
  12473. Extract exact founder issuance date from board action
  12474. Extract consideration language
  12475. Extract vesting or repurchase rights if present
  12476. Update ledger with exact values
  12477. Update cap table with exact values
  12478. Mark founder packet substantially complete
  12479. Leave trust transfer untouched unless separately decided
  12480. Seventh Click Index
  12481. Eighth Click Sequence
  12482. Hunt EIN confirmation letter
  12483. Hunt Delaware franchise tax receipts
  12484. Hunt Delaware annual report receipts
  12485. Confirm Minnesota foreign qualification status
  12486. Confirm Minnesota annual renewal status if applicable
  12487. Update tax calendar and deadline register
  12488. Update missing-file statuses
  12489. Log unresolved tax gaps
  12490. Eighth Click Index
  12491. Final Click Sequence
  12492. Review binder tree for completeness
  12493. Confirm every found file has canonical path
  12494. Confirm every missing file has explicit placeholder
  12495. Confirm every workbook has starter rows
  12496. Confirm duplicates are either resolved or flagged
  12497. Confirm founder stock has ledger and cap table entry
  12498. Confirm trust work remains clearly pending if not executed
  12499. Best-Order Work Queue Master Index
  12500. BlackRoad Best-Order Work Blueprint

  13990. Mirror Class Index
  13991. BlackRoad Classification Protocol
  13992. If it governs the company keep it in Gitea only
  13993. If it runs the platform keep it in Gitea first
  13994. If it explains the platform mirror only after cleanup
  13995. If it contains secrets or sensitive records never mirror
  13996. If it is experimental keep it sandboxed
  13997. If it is archival keep it restorable not public by default
  13998. Classify every repo before syncing

  14985. rollback states get suffix flags
  14986. contradiction states get suffix flags
  14987. review outcomes get suffix flags
  14988. proof allocation review rule
  14989. proof allocation audit rule
  14990. Promotion And Proof Index
  14991. BlackRoad-Portable Protocol
  14992. 15000 becomes the universal local anchor
  14993. every org, repo, file, agent, and atom hangs from it
  14994. every local folder can mirror the numeric structure
  14995. every change can point to a bigger synthesis target
  14996. parallel work scales by address not by branch alone
  14997. the system must remain human-readable
  14998. the system must remain machine-indexable
  14999. Address Space Master Index

  15091. BlackRoad-Portable Folder Protocol
  15092. use 15000 as the universal root
  15093. let orgs, repos, files, agents, and atoms each have stable ranges
  15094. keep human-readable names next to numeric anchors
  15095. let every future repo and file slot into this tree
  15096. use crosswalk files instead of silent renames
  15097. let parallel agents write atoms independently
  15098. synthesize upward from atoms into repos and orgs

  16290. Control Register Index
  16291. BlackRoad Universal Register Protocol
  16292. every major layer gets its own register
  16293. every register lives under 15910-REGISTERS
  16294. every register row must carry numeric address context
  16295. every rename must write to crosswalk before cleanup
  16296. every promotion must update state registers
  16297. every archive event must update recovery registers
  16298. every layer must stay machine-queryable
  16299. Universal Register Master Index
  16300. BlackRoad Universal Register Blueprint

  16611. 15011-Root-Map.md Starter
  16612. # BlackRoad Universal Root Map
  16613. Purpose: define the 15000-series address space as the local universal map for orgs, repos, files, agents,
     atoms, proof, merge, promotion, archive, and control.
  16614. Root: /Applications/BlackRoad-Portable/15000-BlackRoad-Universal
  16615. Primary Layers: 15100 ORGS | 15200 REPOS | 15300 FILES | 15400 AGENTS | 15500 ATOMS | 15600 PROOF | 15700
     MERGE | 15800 PROMOTION | 15900 ARCHIVE
  16616. Canonical Rule: this tree is addressable, portable, and crosswalk-friendly.
  16617. Review Status: Draft
  16618. Owner: Roadie
  16619. Last Review: 2026-04-09
  16620. Root Map Index
  16621. 15012-Address-Space-Rules.md Starter
  16622. # Address Space Rules
  16623. Every org, repo, file, agent, and change atom gets a stable numeric anchor.
  16624. Numeric anchors must not be silently reused.
  16625. Old names survive through crosswalks, aliases, and supersession registers.
  16626. Human-readable labels should sit beside numeric anchors.
  16627. The system must support local-first work, Gitea canonicality, and public mirrors as downstream copies
     only.
  16628. Unknown values must be marked Pending.
  16629. All promotions must remain reversible.
  16630. Address Space Rules Index
  16631. 15013-Org-Allocation-Table.md Starter

  16661. 15016-Change-Atom-Rules.md Starter
  16662. # Change Atom Rules
  16663. One atom = one atomic contribution.
  16664. Every atom must have intent, target, proof path, and current state.
  16665. Atoms should be promotable independently.
  16666. Atoms should be rollback-safe independently.
  16667. Atoms should link upward to goals and tasks.
  16668. Atoms should not rely on branch names alone for identity.
  16669. Atoms must remain addressable in the 15500 layer.
  16670. Change Atom Rules Index
  16671. 15017-Proof-Rules.md Starter
  16672. # Proof Rules
  16673. Every promoted contribution needs proof.
  16674. Proof types include text, file, diff, screenshot, log, test, review, and external source.
  16675. Proof must map to a claim or atom.
  16676. Proof must carry source, date, and reviewer or validator where possible.
  16677. Proof should be both human-readable and machine-indexable.
  16678. Proof should survive rollback and supersession.
  16679. Proof lives in the 15600 layer.
  16680. Proof Rules Index
  16681. 15018-Promotion-Rules.md Starter
  16682. # Promotion Rules
  16683. Nothing becomes canonical silently.
  16684. Promotion requires passing gates for intent, proof, dependencies, contradictions, and review.
  16685. Mirrors are downstream of canonicals.
  16686. Superseded canonicals remain traceable.
  16687. Rollback is first-class.
  16688. Promotion state must be queryable across the local portable system.
  16689. Promotion lives in the 15800 layer.
  16690. Promotion Rules Index
  16691. Register Placeholder Content Rule
  16692. 15111-Org-Register.xlsx starts with header row plus starter rows for the 8 canonical Gitea orgs.
  16693. 15211-Canonical-Repo-Register.xlsx starts with header row plus starter rows for the first 8 canonical
     repos.
  16694. 15311-Canonical-File-Register.xlsx starts with header row plus starter rows for the canonical
     incorporation, equity, and tax files already found.
  16695. 15411-Agent-Register.xlsx starts with header row plus starter rows for the first 8 assigned Roadies.
  16696. 15511-Atom-Register.xlsx starts with header row plus starter rows for binder and equity setup tasks.
  16697. 15611-Proof-Register.xlsx starts with header row and placeholder proof rows only after first atoms exist.
  16698. 15711-Merge-Graph-Register.xlsx starts empty except header until first graph links are recorded.

  16891. Queue State Rules
  16892. move ticket out of inbox once scoped
  16893. move ticket to ready only when actionable
  16894. move ticket to waiting-on-document only for external fact gaps
  16895. move ticket to waiting-on-review only for decision gates
  16896. move ticket to blocked only if dependency truly blocks progress
  16897. move ticket to completed only with proof
  16898. move ticket to archived only after completion is preserved

  16910. Queue Ticket Template Index
  16911. Universal Ticket Header
  16912. [TICKET ID]: TKT-[DOMAIN]-[SEQ]
  16913. [ADDRESS]: 15000/15100/15200/15300-linked target
  16914. [TITLE]: short actionable title
  16915. [STATE]: Inbox / Ready / In Progress / Waiting On Document / Waiting On Review / Blocked / Completed /
     Archived
  16916. [PRIORITY]: Critical / High / Medium / Low
  16917. [OWNER]: named Roadie or human
  16918. [CREATED]: YYYY-MM-DD
  16919. [LAST UPDATED]: YYYY-MM-DD
  16920. Universal Ticket Header Index
  16921. Universal Ticket Body
  16922. [GOAL]: parent goal ID or summary
  16923. [TASK]: concrete task summary
  16924. [SOURCE PATHS]: list source files or systems
  16925. [TARGET PATHS]: list canonical destinations
  16926. [DEPENDENCIES]: blocking facts, files, or decisions
  16927. [COMPLETION CRITERIA]: objective done condition
  16928. [PROOF REQUIRED]: what evidence closes the ticket
  16929. [NEXT HANDOFF]: where output goes next
  16930. Universal Ticket Body Index
  16931. Notes And Review Section
  16932. [NOTES]: explicit unresolved items
  16933. [REVIEWER]: assigned reviewer if required
  16934. [REVIEW STATUS]: Pending / Approved / Rejected / Needs Changes
  16935. [CONTRADICTIONS]: linked contradiction IDs if any
  16936. [PROMOTION TARGET]: canonical state if completed
  16937. [ROLLBACK PATH]: reversal path if needed
  16938. [CROSSWALKS]: old names/paths affected
  16939. [QUEUE LOCATION]: actual queue folder path
  16940. Notes And Review Index
